## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes API Deprecation Policy Enforcement

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that enforce the API deprecation policy: the deprecated API version warning injection, the removal version validation, and the minimum supported API version checks in the API server.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources


## API Deprecation Policy Enforcement in Kubernetes

The enforcement spans three main areas:

### 1. Deprecated API Version Warning Injection
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go`** — Core logic: `IsDeprecated()`, `WarningMessage()`, `RemovedRelease()`, `MajorMinor()`
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go`** — At route registration, calls the deprecation functions and wraps handlers with `AddWarningsHandler`
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go`** — `AddWarningsHandler` injects warning strings per request
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/warning/context.go`** — `AddWarning()` context-level recording
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/warning.go`** — `WithWarningRecorder` HTTP middleware that writes RFC 2616 `Warning: 299` response headers

### 2. Removal Version Validation / Minimum Supported API Version
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go`** — `ResourceExpirationEvaluator`, `ShouldServeForVersion()`, `RemoveDeletedKinds()` — removes expired API groups at startup
- **`pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go`** — calls `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator` to enforce removal at server startup

### 3. Metrics Recording
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go`** — `deprecatedRequestGauge` (`apiserver_requested_deprecated_apis`), `MonitorRequest()`, `InstrumentRouteFunc()` — records metrics and audit annotations for deprecated API calls

### Supporting
- **CRD deprecation**: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` and `validation/validation.go`
- **Code generator**: `staging/src/k8s

Core Deprecation Logic\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go` is the central file. It defines:\\n- `IsDeprecated(obj, currentMajor, currentMinor)`: checks if an object implements `APILifecycleDeprecated()` and whether the deprecation version is <= current server version\\n- `RemovedRelease(obj)`: extracts the removal version string (e.g. \\\"1.25\\\") from `APILifecycleRemoved()`\\n- `WarningMessage(obj)`: builds the human-readable deprecation warning string\\n- `MajorMinor(versionInfo)`: parses the current server version\\n\\n## 2. Warning Injection at Request Handling\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go` wires the deprecation system into route registration. For each API resource route, it calls `deprecation.IsDeprecated`, `deprecation.RemovedRelease`, `deprecation.WarningMessage`, then passes warnings to `AddWarningsHandler` and the deprecated/removedRelease flags to `metrics.InstrumentRouteFunc`.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go` provides `AddWarningsHandler`, which wraps route handlers to inject deprecation warnings into the response context on every request.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/warning/context.go` provides `AddWarning(ctx, agent, text)`, the low-level function that records a warning to the context Recorder.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/warning.go` provides `WithWarningRecorder`, an HTTP middleware that attaches a deduplicating recorder to each request context and writes RFC 2616 `Warning: 299` headers to the HTTP response.\\n\\n## 3. Metrics Recording for Deprecated APIs\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go` defines:\\n- `deprecatedRequestGauge` (`apiserver_requested_deprecated_apis`): a stable Prometheus GaugeVec tracking deprecated API usage by group/version/resource/subresource/removed_release\\n- `MonitorRequest`: sets the gauge and adds audit annotations (`k8s.io/deprecated=true`, `k8s.io/removed-release=<X.Y>`) for deprecated requests\\n- `InstrumentRouteFunc` / `InstrumentHandlerFunc`: wraps handlers to call `MonitorRequest` after each request\\n\\n## 4. Removal Version Validation / Minimum Supported API Version\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go` removes expired API versions from the API server at startup:\\n- `ResourceExpirationEvaluator` interface\\n- `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator(currentVersion)`: creates an evaluator from the current server version, reading env vars `KUBE_APISERVER_STRICT_REMOVED_API_HANDLING_IN_ALPHA` and `KUBE_APISERVER_SERVE_REMOVED_APIS_FOR_ONE_RELEASE`\\n- `ShouldServeForVersion(majorRemoved, minorRemoved)`: returns false when removal version <= current version (the minimum supported version check)\\n- `RemoveDeletedKinds(groupName, versioner, storageMap)`: removes resources whose `APILifecycleRemoved()` version has passed\\n\\n`pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go` calls `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator` and passes it through `InstallAPIs`, which calls `RemoveDeletedKinds` on each API group's storage map before installation.\\n\\n## 5. CRD-Specific Deprecation Enforcement\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` handles deprecation for Custom Resource Definitions. It checks the `Deprecated` and `DeprecationWarning` fields on each CRD version and injects warnings via `warning.AddWarning`.\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go` validates CRD deprecation fields via `validateDeprecationWarning`, ensuring `DeprecationWarning` is only set when `Deprecated=true`.\\n\\n## 6. API Lifecycle Code Generator\\n\\n`staging/src/k8s.io/code-generator/cmd/prerelease-lifecycle-gen/prerelease-lifecycle-generators/status.go` and `main.go` implement the `prerelease-lifecycle-gen` tool. It processes `+k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:deprecated=X.Y` and `+k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:removed=X.Y` tags to auto-generate `APILifecycleDeprecated()`, `APILifecycleRemoved()`, `APILifecycleIntroduced()`, and `APILifecycleReplacement()` methods in `zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go` files across all API packages.\\n\\n## 7. Generated Lifecycle Implementations\\n\\nThe actual deprecation/removal version data is stored in generated files:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/networking/v1alpha1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/networking/v1beta1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1beta1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/admissionregistration/v1alpha1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/admissionregistration/v1beta1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/events/v1beta1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/node/v1beta1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/coordination/v1alpha2/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/apidiscovery/v2beta1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/certificates/v1alpha1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/storagemigration/v1alpha1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/storage/v1alpha1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/policy/v1beta1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/authentication/v1beta1/zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go`\\n\\nThese implement the `APILifecycleDeprecated()` and `APILifecycleRemoved()` interfaces consumed by the enforcement code above.\"\n}\n",
